White poker #21w42

1. The project brings its own white paper;
2. Players read and express their personal subjective opinion about the project from the point of view of an investor, developer, etc. for example: yes/no ‚Äî explanation ‚Äî one, two sentences, or abstract;
3. To avoid the anchoring effect for more details see Planning Poker, the player hashed his solution and publishes the hash;
4. At the appointed time, everyone opens up and considers the results.

In reply to this message
It's not just any one thing. There are projects and integrations being worked on that will do a lot. If you guys can't come to the weekly community calls, I understand, but most of the plans are discussed there. Just scroll through the YouTube page to see what's in the pipeline.

At the same time, you guys and gals are all (mostly I guess) developers. You know how long some things take. I don't want to keep saying "soon", but if I say "this and this date" you'll only hold my feet to the fire.

We spend day and night, weekends and holidays busting our asses in work. You know that, I'm sure. But please don't expect things to happen with the speed of a finger snap. I wrote this comment November 19. Considering that it's Jan 24 with the holidays in between, that's a finger snap. Nothing happens that fast, folks.

There's Flex in the works. Numiz. KWPC and KW Finance. QAN. Evercraft. The DeFi Alliance has a buuuunch of stuff rolling out. I can go on forever. There's boosted staking in Surf. I mean there's a lot of stuff. How soon? As soon as they're ready. 2022 is a packed year, that's for sure. But I cannot commit to dates. You all know that.

Thanks for keeping me on my toes though :)
